  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d0b47f5e-7257-4577-8fb2-1b87a7ffd063'
      });

  <span id="freeText15867439992042813504" style="display:none">It bites: New York hotels cost an arm and a leg, and Terri had flown from England to help plan her cousin’s wedding. The new in-laws offered lodging. But they were a weird bunch. There was the sometimes-chipper-sometimes-brooding Lucern, and the wacky stage-actor, Vincent. (She couldn't imagine Broadway casting a hungrier singing-and-dancing Dracula.) And then there was Bastien. Just looking into his eyes, Terri had to admit she was falling for him - someone even taller, darker and hungrier than the other two. She was feeling a mite peckish herself. And if she stayed with him, those blood-sucking hotel owners wouldn't get to her!</span>

        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });

<span id="freeTextContainer5294292832655847584"><b>3 only for Bastien Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/9015270_zps9prdqrcw.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>OMG The last part of this book just pissed me off. I was loving this book. Bastien was so charming. Then Terri pulls some coward ass bs towards the end and bam I am throwing my paperback across the room like a 3 year old in the middle of a melt down! I was so mad I almost 1 stared it out of spite, but I did really really love Bastien soooo. All 3 of my stars are for sexy Bastien. Terri just pissed me off. She was a total coward ass baby. That makes two heroines in a r</span>
  <span id="freeText5294292832655847584" style="display:none"><b>3 only for Bastien Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/9015270_zps9prdqrcw.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474902190ra/20654301.gif" alt=" photo 9015270_zps9prdqrcw.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>OMG The last part of this book just pissed me off. I was loving this book. Bastien was so charming. Then Terri pulls some coward ass bs towards the end and bam I am throwing my paperback across the room like a 3 year old in the middle of a melt down! I was so mad I almost 1 stared it out of spite, but I did really really love Bastien soooo. All 3 of my stars are for sexy Bastien. Terri just pissed me off. She was a total coward ass baby. That makes two heroines in a row now that have, towards the end of the book, jumped to the wrong conclusion. Then they both jumped planes leaving the heroes high and dry like cowards. In the last book Kate did the same thing. Two books in a row now where the heroine could have very easily asked one question and cleared everything up, but instead like a cowardly baby ran. And it's two books in a row now where after the heroes chased down the cowardly heroines and not only cleared things up but also tell them "I love you and marry me" to have the heroines turn around and say that they need time to think. And then take weeks, to think and still needing a push of someone coming and talking sense into them.<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/8571047_zpsvjvn11ug.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474902190ra/20654302.gif" alt=" photo 8571047_zpsvjvn11ug.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And all I have to say to that shit is this better not be the pattern of the series. I have a huge pet peeve with cowards and I just went through hell with a 20 book series filled with nothing but cowards from Susan Mallery that I didn't think I would survive!!!! I swear to God if this series pulls a Susan Mallery "Fools Gold series" and they all start doing the damn chicken dance being cowards, I am going to be soooo pissed. No strike that I am already pissed at this heroine and the last one. I am going to lose my shit. Please don't let this be a pattern! Below I leave a quote from the Terri's sister-n-law because I loved how she called her out on her cowardly ass bs!<br><br><b>"Everything you've told me about him tells me that. And here you are, hurting both him and yourself, for no good reason other than you're a coward. It takes courage to live, Terri. To really live. To follow your dreams, to love someone, to face each day. Agoraphobics are trapped in their homes because they are terrified of what might happen--but as long as they stay inside, they'll never know what could happen. You're an emotional agoraphobic. You've been one since Ian died, avoiding emotional entanglements to avoid getting hurt. Well, it's high time you rejoined the living, my girl, and stopped acting like you're the one in the cold hard grave. I bet Ian would give anything to be alive and in love, yet here you have it and you're throwing it away." -Sandi</b><br></span>

<div id="review_3405613877" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3405613877" />
    <a title="John" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74160709-john"><img alt="John" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/m_50x66-82093808bca726cb3249a493fbd3bd0f.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3405613877?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="John" class="user" itemprop="url" name="John" href="/user/show/74160709-john">John</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74160709-john?shelf=owned">owned</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3405613877" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10533078511130891101">This fourth installment of the Argeneau series tells how Bastien gets together with his life mate Terri Simpson. He's the last of the four siblings to do so, both chronologically and in the recommended reading order; it's just a historical oddity now that the first four books were published in a different order (in terms of chronology #3 came out first, then #2, then #4--that's this one--and finally #1). <br/><br/>This, of course, means that Marguerite Argeneau will no longer play the role of the interven</span>
  <span id="freeText10533078511130891101" style="display:none">This fourth installment of the Argeneau series tells how Bastien gets together with his life mate Terri Simpson. He's the last of the four siblings to do so, both chronologically and in the recommended reading order; it's just a historical oddity now that the first four books were published in a different order (in terms of chronology #3 came out first, then #2, then #4--that's this one--and finally #1). <br /><br />This, of course, means that Marguerite Argeneau will no longer play the role of the intervening mother; she'll have to be the intervening aunt or cousin or something else, but she's such a bright spot in each book I hope she'll continue to intervene. Lord knows these nice single vampires need that.<br /><br />It's still comfort reading, and the whole series gets an extra half star from me because of Lynsay Sands's brilliant idea: scientists in Atlantis long ago developed self-replicating nanobots to inject into people to heal injuries and it turned out they did more than that--they heal diseases and vastly lengthen lifespans, and they're passed along to offspring. All they need to do their jobs is a bit of blood from time to time, or they'll use up the person's own blood.<br /><br />Unfortunately, you really need to have read at least one of the previous books in the series to grasp what these characters are all about. Here you're just plunged into their everyday lifestyle and you learn what their needs, powers, and limitations are as they come up in the story, with no explanation of why it's like that until the very end. That's not the only reason, though, why my rating has dropped from four to three stars.<br /><br />It's a personal thing, humor. And for me the humor has gone from laugh-out-loud in #3 to mildly amusing for the most part here in #4. Some of the other readers found the mishaps of planning an elaborate wedding much funnier than I did, and some of the truly comic moments had a serious undertone <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[for example, the caterer commits suicide and they have to choose a new one <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>--I guess it's no spoiler that Chris, the bride's colleague and a character I really want to see more of, is in so many scenes because he has to be rushed to the hospital so often. Even so, Chris provides good comedy, unlike Bastien's cousin Vincent. Again, Vincent delighted quite a few readers, but I didn't care for him--he came across to me as a rather spoiled smart-ass, and a lot of his scenes were more irritating than funny.<br /><br />And this is a paranormal romance, even if the paranormal part of it is basically science fiction (nanobots! feed them! but you don't know that till the end). So the happy ending is an absolute necessity for the reader, even if it comes as a surprise to the characters. And in this one our lovers, Bastien and Terri, immediately develop intense feelings for each other, which they express in many meticulously described sex scenes. The one that lasts 20 pages goes all the way in every sense, but most of the others end with comic interruptions. So if "steamy stuff" isn't for you, just skip through to a possible laugh.<br /><br />The basic plot, then, is for the lovers to figure out if their instant lust is also instant love. To make that a novel instead of a very short story, we need a series of Romantic Misunderstandings. We certainly get them, and some of them are rather amusing. But we also get page after page of each lover's Romantic Uncertainty--you know, pulling the petals off the metaphoric dandelion, loves me, loves me not--and here I began to suspect the publisher required a longer word count than the author could easily muster.<br /><br />Then Romantic Misunderstandings and Romantic Uncertainty deepen into Romantic Stupidity and even Romantic Cowardice, requiring the intervention of virtually all the other characters to make it possible for the climactic Romantic Scramble to happen (involving airports of course!) and yield the Happy Ending. Sorry, the stupid part just didn't ring true. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[If you hear someone hint that your sex partner and major heartthrob might have a terminal illness, wouldn't you go to your loved one immediately and find out if that's for real? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />The writing style made for easy reading and I liked most of the characters (even when they were being stupid), so for me this book was better than just "okay"--I rather enjoyed it for the most part.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10533078511130891101" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3419439523854371504"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487561375i/22026357.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Reviewed for <a href='http://www.herdingcats-burningsoup.com/2017/05/tall-dark-and-hungry-by-lynsay-sands.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>herding cats & burning soup</a>.<br/>Amazon: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/2lZ1w92'>http://amzn.to/2lZ1w92</a><br/><br/>So. First off. This series? Totally can read out of order. I started with book 19. Then came to book 4. Totally fine. No worries. <br/><br/>The Story: <br/><br/>I had a lot of fun with Tall, Dark & Hungry. It's a bit madcap with the hero and heroine trying to save a wedding of their family/friend and dealing with blunder after blunder after disaster. From wedding favor disasters to finding a new caterer and flowers and on and on. It's rather sil</span>
  <span id="freeText3419439523854371504" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487561375i/22026357.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Reviewed for <a href="http://www.herdingcats-burningsoup.com/2017/05/tall-dark-and-hungry-by-lynsay-sands.html" rel="nofollow noopener">herding cats &amp; burning soup</a>.<br>Amazon: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2lZ1w92">http://amzn.to/2lZ1w92</a><br><br>So. First off. This series? Totally can read out of order. I started with book 19. Then came to book 4. Totally fine. No worries. <br><br>The Story: <br><br>I had a lot of fun with Tall, Dark &amp; Hungry. It's a bit madcap with the hero and heroine trying to save a wedding of their family/friend and dealing with blunder after blunder after disaster. From wedding favor disasters to finding a new caterer and flowers and on and on. It's rather silly but quite entertaining. As was watching the sassy British heroine fall for our vampire hero. They were cute together. Had some nice heat and laughs and worked well as a team. Both were easy to like and cheer for.<br><br>The Narration:<br><br>The narration worked. Jeffrey Cummings did a nice job creating distinction between the characters and giving accents where accents were due. The female voices took a little getting used to but not more than a couple chapters and after that I listened to this 9 hour audio in record time. 3ish days? Something like that which is fast for me. He made the silly antics and disasters quite humorous and the steamy scenes which can be a miss on audio for me weren't bad either. I'd listen to him again no problem. I listened on regular 1.0x setting which is slower than I usually listen at but fit his voice and pacing.</span>

<div id="review_1690773405" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1690773405" />
    <a title="Elaine Howlin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5214040-elaine-howlin"><img alt="Elaine Howlin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517160215p2/5214040.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2050342529?book_show_action=true">Jul 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Umaiya ❄️Ramblings of a Scattered Mind❄️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Umaiya ❄️Ramblings of a Scattered Mind❄️" href="/user/show/7517714-umaiya-ramblings-of-a-scattered-mind">Umaiya ❄️Ramblings of a Scattered Mind❄️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780843963441" href="/book/show/6681585-tall-dark-hungry">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7517714-umaiya-ramblings-of-a-scattered-mind?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7517714-umaiya-ramblings-of-a-scattered-mind?shelf=fangs">fangs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7517714-umaiya-ramblings-of-a-scattered-mind?shelf=insta-insta-insta">insta-insta-insta</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2050342529" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17536189218074751494"><br/>I think I liked this one best of the four. Lol, it's entirely possible I said this about the last one too :P<br/>Anyway, I liked Terri and I loved how this had real life moments from Sands own life, seemed more personal. <br/>Here's something that's been bugging me throughout the series. First, the insta. I'm an insta fan but it's getting on my nerves. I want them to put some actual work into it. I get all the MCs especially the Argeneau's are supposed to be gorgeous but there's more to love than a pretty</span>
  <span id="freeText17536189218074751494" style="display:none"><br />I think I liked this one best of the four. Lol, it's entirely possible I said this about the last one too :P<br />Anyway, I liked Terri and I loved how this had real life moments from Sands own life, seemed more personal. <br />Here's something that's been bugging me throughout the series. First, the insta. I'm an insta fan but it's getting on my nerves. I want them to put some actual work into it. I get all the MCs especially the Argeneau's are supposed to be gorgeous but there's more to love than a pretty face.<br />Second, the perfect-fit, tailor made mate thing that's going on. I swear they're starting to feel like the male/female version of the other. They like the same books, games, food, even have the same opinions. I'm sorry, I re]ealize that's supposed to make it romantic but it just comes off as fake and unreal instead. <br />You're probably thinking, <i>It's a Vampire novel and their sameness is what seems unreal? *scoffs*</i> <br />I know but I mean their relationship, the one between the man and the woman, comes off unnatural.<br />That being said, it's not that the book wasn't any good cause it was. It had some real lol moments like the others and I think it's entirely possible the series gets better the further in you get cause every time I think I'm getting tired of it, it springs another character whose story I'd be interested I finding out. *shrugs* <br />Hazarding a guess here but Vincent's probably next up. <br />*sigh*<br />To read or not to read, that is the question.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17536189218074751494" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1502503056492014896">I think this has been my favorite of the books in this series so far. Sure it was a series of unfortunate events happening to other people that kept throwing our couple together, but it was amusing because of it. I felt bad for Chris though. That poor guy had every bad thing possible happening to him. How many times could they end up in the hospital for stupid random accidents. But it did keep Terri and Bastien having to deal with crisis after crisis. I liked that through it all Bastien kept fin</span>
  <span id="freeText1502503056492014896" style="display:none">I think this has been my favorite of the books in this series so far. Sure it was a series of unfortunate events happening to other people that kept throwing our couple together, but it was amusing because of it. I felt bad for Chris though. That poor guy had every bad thing possible happening to him. How many times could they end up in the hospital for stupid random accidents. But it did keep Terri and Bastien having to deal with crisis after crisis. I liked that through it all Bastien kept finding ways to romance Terri and create fun dates for them without being overt about it. <br /><br />Vincent cracked me up in this story and I'm not sure if I remember reading his book or not. I'm actually looking forward to his story. It should be fun. :)<br /><br />Then ending of this story was predictable in its' misunderstanding, but still was satisfying in the way that it revolved. I knew Terri was going to have her freak out moment, but of course it was over her assumptions first rather than reality. </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer82857449" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14422503234061218368">I'm giving this book two stars, because while it was good, it was not one of the best things I've ever read. It didn't get interesting for me until after the first couple hundred pages. And, that being said, it only seemed to get more interesting because they had sex and finally things were starting to get exciting. I didn't really like everything that happened in the last couple chapters; it kinda pissed me off. I just didn't like this book as much as I was expecting to. When I read the back of</span>
  <span id="freeText14422503234061218368" style="display:none">I'm giving this book two stars, because while it was good, it was not one of the best things I've ever read. It didn't get interesting for me until after the first couple hundred pages. And, that being said, it only seemed to get more interesting because they had sex and finally things were starting to get exciting. I didn't really like everything that happened in the last couple chapters; it kinda pissed me off. I just didn't like this book as much as I was expecting to. When I read the back of it in the store, it sounded really good. And, also, I've read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/17059.Lynsay_Sands" title="Lynsay Sands" rel="nofollow noopener">Lynsay Sands</a>' <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1422253.The_Accidental_Vampire__Argeneau___7_" title="The Accidental Vampire (Argeneau, #7) by Lynsay Sands" rel="nofollow noopener">The Accidental Vampire</a> previously and was expecting this book to be good like that one was.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14422503234061218368" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_94332582" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/94332582" />
    <a title="DarienMoya" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3069494-darienmoya"><img alt="DarienMoya" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536718485p2/3069494.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/94332582?book_show_action=true">Mar 16, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="DarienMoya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="DarienMoya" href="/user/show/3069494-darienmoya">DarienMoya</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780843963441" href="/book/show/6681585-tall-dark-hungry">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3069494-darienmoya?shelf=2010-reads">2010-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3069494-darienmoya?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer94332582" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13143466204912903010">TALL,DARK AND MEDIOCRE!!!<br/>The fourth book in the Argeneau series is one fun ride. While not being able to live up to the genius that is Single White Vampire, the book is still able to capture your attention and manages to introduce some fun characters. Plus you get tabs on old characters and that in it self is just awesome. Recap this series is about a family of Canadian vampires and their search for love.<br/><br/>Bastien is the second oldest of Argeneau children and the most take charge. He is in charge </span>
  <span id="freeText13143466204912903010" style="display:none">TALL,DARK AND MEDIOCRE!!!<br />The fourth book in the Argeneau series is one fun ride. While not being able to live up to the genius that is Single White Vampire, the book is still able to capture your attention and manages to introduce some fun characters. Plus you get tabs on old characters and that in it self is just awesome. Recap this series is about a family of Canadian vampires and their search for love.<br /><br />Bastien is the second oldest of Argeneau children and the most take charge. He is in charge of the family business, and he is the go to guy when you need something done. So as you can probably tell he hardly has time for himself much less time to find love. Plus he has some reluctance when it comes to love, once being in love with a human female and being completely rejected his faith in love has been shaken. Can someone really fall in love with what he is. Seems that luck is on his side, and might have found a mate in his sister-in-law’s cousin when she appears to help plan the wedding between Lucern and Kate ( check Single White Vampire). Seems that all business and no play Bastien is about to shake things up. So he’s no longer a dull boy.<br /><br />Terri is in New York to help plan her cousins wedding, and the brother of the groom is a dream boat all tall, dark and handsome…… So events lead to Terri staying with Bastien at his penthouse with Bastien’s cousin Vincent, and Kate’s co-worker Chris aka CK. Terri knows what its like to lose a love one to a chronic debilitating illness, and when she finds IV stands, syringes and bags of blood she realizes that Bastien might not be as healthy as he appears. One thing Terri cant do again is watch a man she loves succumb to an illness and die. She does love Bastien and she loves him something fierce. Who would have thought that a trip to plan a wedding would lead to an happily ever-after or a not so happy ending.<br /><br />This book was one disaster after another. Some of the situations was funny when it included CK, what a funny guy. I thought that Terri’s character was a little on the annoying side, way too many mishaps with this one. I did enjoy Bastien though, all cool and collected, mmmmm yummo. Although not my fave of the series I did enjoy reading it because you cant help but get drawn into this wonderful vampiric family antics. A fun light read with a little blood and a nice amount of a laugh plus it Canadian. BING!!!! Just sold it right there.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13143466204912903010" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_199278860" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/199278860" />
    <a title="t&#39;irla ~The Bookslayer~ aka Barbara" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5601870-t-irla-the-bookslayer-aka-barbara"><img alt="t&#39;irla ~The Bookslayer~ aka Barbara" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1507934269p2/5601870.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/199278860?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="t&#39;irla ~The Bookslayer~ aka Barbara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="t&#39;irla ~The Bookslayer~ aka Barbara" href="/user/show/5601870-t-irla-the-bookslayer-aka-barbara">t&#39;irla ~The Bookslayer~ aka Barbara</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5601870-t-irla-the-bookslayer-aka-barbara?shelf=romance-paranormal2">romance-paranormal2</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5601870-t-irla-the-bookslayer-aka-barbara?shelf=4-star-read">4-star-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer199278860" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3442500652216486214">Finally, a story I can get my teeth into!<br/><br/>Description: <br/><br/>It bites: New York hotels cost an arm and a leg, and Terri has flown from England to help plan her cousin’s wedding. The new in-laws offered lodging. But they’re a weird bunch -- and it isn’t just that they’re Canadian! There is the sometimes-chipper-sometimes-silent Lucern, and the wacky stage-actor Vincent: she can’t imagine Broadway casting a hungrier singing-and-dancing Dracula. And then there is Bastien. Just looking into his eyes, Terri</span>
  <span id="freeText3442500652216486214" style="display:none">Finally, a story I can get my teeth into!<br /><br />Description: <br /><br />It bites: New York hotels cost an arm and a leg, and Terri has flown from England to help plan her cousin’s wedding. The new in-laws offered lodging. But they’re a weird bunch -- and it isn’t just that they’re Canadian! There is the sometimes-chipper-sometimes-silent Lucern, and the wacky stage-actor Vincent: she can’t imagine Broadway casting a hungrier singing-and-dancing Dracula. And then there is Bastien. Just looking into his eyes, Terri has to admit she’s falling for someone even taller, darker, and hungrier. She’s feeling a mite peckish herself. And if she stays with him, those bloodsucking hotel owners won’t get her!<br /><br />My Thoughts:<br /><br />So far my favorite of the Argeneau Series LS has finally broken through and created characters that are more than one dimensional. Their personalities are deeper and you can feel them leap off the book at you. In the past books in this series the secondary characters have always been more interesting and more unique than the h/h but although Vincent and C.K. are hilarious I found Bastien and Terri so sweet. I loved that Bastien was sensitive and unsure of himself. I liked that Terri was a bit flighty and said what she was thinking. That being said I couldn't figured out why she stepped out of character and ran near the end of the book. It just didn't fit her forthright personality. I admit to thinking that Bastien was a cold fish in previous books and was so happy to find a hidden depth and sense of humour about him. The story was much more unique than those found in the past books and you now can really get into what set this series apart from other more meh turn outs. Love LS's definition of Vampires and their beginnings. Love the closeness and sense of family she creates in the books. <br /><br />All this said I give this outing a soft 4 stars. But have to admit I'm looking forward to Vincent's book as he was my favorite character to come out of this one. I also can't wait to find out what is going to happen with C.K. cause you just know we will be seeing more of him. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3442500652216486214" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_128077013" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/128077013" />
    <a title="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595947372p2/3108364.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/128077013?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog">Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780843963441" href="/book/show/6681585-tall-dark-hungry">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-paranormal-romance">genre-paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-read-2011">books-read-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-audio-books">read-audio-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer128077013" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17025040950889513877">I'm a bit disappointed! I really like Bastien, and I was hoping his book would be so sexy and he would get the perfect heroine to shake him up! But that's not exactly how I feel after reading this book.<br/><br/>First of all, I felt a lack of the humor that was always present in the past books in this series. I don't think I can recall one moment where I was really laughing like in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/263149.Single_White_Vampire__Argeneau___3_' title='Single White Vampire (Argeneau, #3) by Lynsay Sands' rel='nofollow noopener'>Single White Vampire</a>. Yes, there's some moments you could consider funny, but it wasn't the same.<br/><br/>In this book, Bastien is lef</span>
  <span id="freeText17025040950889513877" style="display:none">I'm a bit disappointed! I really like Bastien, and I was hoping his book would be so sexy and he would get the perfect heroine to shake him up! But that's not exactly how I feel after reading this book.<br /><br />First of all, I felt a lack of the humor that was always present in the past books in this series. I don't think I can recall one moment where I was really laughing like in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/263149.Single_White_Vampire__Argeneau___3_" title="Single White Vampire (Argeneau, #3) by Lynsay Sands" rel="nofollow noopener">Single White Vampire</a>. Yes, there's some moments you could consider funny, but it wasn't the same.<br /><br />In this book, Bastien is left to entertain Kate's cousin from England, while Kate and Lucern go take care of her work. At the same time, they have to save Lucern and Kate's wedding, as all plans fall apart. It was just one catastrophe after another!<br /><br />My main complaint is that I never felt the connection between Terri and Bastien. Maybe the story would've been better if we got to see more the Argeneau family! They were absent for the most part.<br /><br />It's a light read, with some humor, no action, plenty of wedding drama, and though not the best in this series, it's an enjoyable book. </span>
  <a data-text-id="17025040950889513877" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2334831210" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2334831210" />
    <a title="Connie N." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3154417-connie-n"><img alt="Connie N." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346895307p2/3154417.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2334831210?book_show_action=true">Jun 17, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Connie N." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Connie N." href="/user/show/3154417-connie-n">Connie N.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3154417-connie-n?shelf=sweets-on-cover">sweets-on-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3154417-connie-n?shelf=white">white</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3154417-connie-n?shelf=audio-audible">audio-audible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3154417-connie-n?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3154417-connie-n?shelf=paranormal-vampires">paranormal-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3154417-connie-n?shelf=4th-in-series">4th-in-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3154417-connie-n?shelf=narr-jeffrey-cummings">narr-jeffrey-cummings</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2334831210" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2943433626212847705">#4 in the Argeneau paranormal romance series<br/><br/>When Terry comes to NY early before her cousin Kate's wedding to Luke, she gets thrown together with Bastion unexpectedly. As always with this series, there are a number of hilariously over-the-top incidents involving Bastion's housekeeper, his cousin Vincent, and Kate's friend CK. When a couple of crazy calamities also occur regarding the upcoming wedding, Bastion and Terry have to make some decisions while Kate and Luke are away. As they deal with al</span>
  <span id="freeText2943433626212847705" style="display:none">#4 in the Argeneau paranormal romance series<br /><br />When Terry comes to NY early before her cousin Kate's wedding to Luke, she gets thrown together with Bastion unexpectedly. As always with this series, there are a number of hilariously over-the-top incidents involving Bastion's housekeeper, his cousin Vincent, and Kate's friend CK. When a couple of crazy calamities also occur regarding the upcoming wedding, Bastion and Terry have to make some decisions while Kate and Luke are away. As they deal with all these issues, their attraction for each other grows, but there is always a suspicion on Terry's part that Bastion has some kind of medical condition because of the clues she's discovering. And after having dealt with her husband's death, she can't face another medical problem so she's holding back. It doesn't have the totally hilarious scenes that we found between Lucern and Kate, but it's close. And the characters are charming and make me smile. Cummings does a fine job of narration. Although his female voicing is not quite right, he does a great job with all of the various male voices which makes it easy to keep track of everyone. He has some great inflections that really add a lot of spark to the story. I look forward to hearing more in this series--they are always good for a laugh and some hot romance.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2943433626212847705" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5691824064657119793">ive been going back and rereading books i read when i was much younger. many of them are quite awful unlike what i remembered. and i am so happy to say that this series is not on of them. you can clearly see the writers talent growwith each novel. <br/>pros:the characterss, were great with solid backstories and understandable realistic motives and emotions. terri osnt as feisty as i normally like my heroines but her directness is lile mine and made up for that. bastien is a workholic after a failed r</span>
  <span id="freeText5691824064657119793" style="display:none">ive been going back and rereading books i read when i was much younger. many of them are quite awful unlike what i remembered. and i am so happy to say that this series is not on of them. you can clearly see the writers talent growwith each novel. <br />pros:the characterss, were great with solid backstories and understandable realistic motives and emotions. terri osnt as feisty as i normally like my heroines but her directness is lile mine and made up for that. bastien is a workholic after a failed relationship but comes to realize what true love is. through a series of unfortunate evens...no really...<br />unfortunate-the two are thrown together and gain a new lease on life. sex scenes were super steamy compared to previous books and the romance was very well developed. though dsappointing that thomas made no appearance in this book comedic relief wasprovided by another family member.<br />cons: i wouldve liked a brief epilogue i know the couple usually ends up getting married in the next book but a little more wouldnt hurt esp if someone doesnt want to read the next one it leaves for an unsatisfying end. also with all the calamities i wanted to find some bigger reason behind them. a couple would be roll your eye at the funny ridiculousness but with that many things gone wrong it feels much less coincidental and id have liked to see a scapegoat...marguerite wouldve been perfect with all her meddling</span>

<div id="review_216877258" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/216877258" />
    <a title="Brandi Salazar" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5366885-brandi-salazar"><img alt="Brandi Salazar" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1304431850p2/5366885.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/216877258?book_show_action=true">Sep 29, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi Salazar" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi Salazar" href="/user/show/5366885-brandi-salazar">Brandi Salazar</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer216877258" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7025245097055208589">This book revolves around a romance between Bastien Argeneau and Terri (insert forgotten last name here--the best man and maid of honor in Lucern (Bastien's brother) and Kate's (Terri's best friend) wedding. Upon her unexpected early arrival, Terri is pushed on Bastien who is forced to give her room and board in his penthouse (not that it was any inconvenience), and they have an immediate attraction to one another. <br/><br/>I found the story quite funny, especially with Vincent's (another Argeneau brothe</span>
  <span id="freeText7025245097055208589" style="display:none">This book revolves around a romance between Bastien Argeneau and Terri (insert forgotten last name here--the best man and maid of honor in Lucern (Bastien's brother) and Kate's (Terri's best friend) wedding. Upon her unexpected early arrival, Terri is pushed on Bastien who is forced to give her room and board in his penthouse (not that it was any inconvenience), and they have an immediate attraction to one another. <br /><br />I found the story quite funny, especially with Vincent's (another Argeneau brother) antics and Kate's friend, co-worker, and editor C.K. who just can't seem to catch a break as a terrible stream of bad luck hits him from every direction, leaving Bastien and Terri to clean up the mess...and get even closer in the process. <br /><br />I like this series a lot, not because it is terribly complicated, but because it has one basic detail to work around and Sands does so in a very romantic way. The Argeneau family may be "vampires" but not so much in the classic vampire definition. But that's a discussion for another time. In my opinion, Sands weaves a lovely tale (with each installment to the Argeneau series) of love in a very straight forward way that gives me the warm and fuzzies and always leaves me wanting more.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7025245097055208589" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer9897373586563019356">Kate's (from previous book Single White Vampire) cousin and best friend Terri is flying into town to help out with Kates wedding. Kate and Lucern ask Lucerns brother Bastien to put Terri up in the penthouse owned by the family and suddenly Terri finds her self stranded with Bastien and his unplanned house guests: His cousin Vincent and Kate's co-editor Chris when Kate is assigned to an out of town writing conference.<br/><br/>A lot of laugh out loud scenes in the book almost from the very begining when Te</span>
  <span id="freeText9897373586563019356" style="display:none">Kate's (from previous book Single White Vampire) cousin and best friend Terri is flying into town to help out with Kates wedding. Kate and Lucern ask Lucerns brother Bastien to put Terri up in the penthouse owned by the family and suddenly Terri finds her self stranded with Bastien and his unplanned house guests: His cousin Vincent and Kate's co-editor Chris when Kate is assigned to an out of town writing conference.<br /><br />A lot of laugh out loud scenes in the book almost from the very begining when Terri greets Bastien confusing him for Lucern because Kate told Terri Lucern would be the most handsome man in the room when she met him on to when Chris the friendly editor is in accident after accident causing him to be hospitalized.<br /><br />There are some sad scenes in this book as well. We learn that Terri had a husband who died and she is very relucant to get into another relationship. In fact, for a while she believes Bastian is ill as well due to his inability to be in sun light for very long and the IV stand she found in his room.<br /><br />Bastien and Terri are one my favorite book couples.<br /><br />Melissa<br /> <br />Reviewer for <a href="http://www.1000plusbookstoread.com" rel="nofollow noopener">1000 + Books to Read</a></span>

<div id="review_159605193" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/159605193" />
    <a title="Samantha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5238046-samantha"><img alt="Samantha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548068787p2/5238046.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/159605193?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Samantha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Samantha" href="/user/show/5238046-samantha">Samantha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5238046-samantha?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer159605193" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12428149646513495419">Really all my feelings on this book can be summed up in one large groan. I had been looking forward to reading about Bastien too. Bastien really could've been an interesting character, but Sands made him out to be a soft snuggle bunny with fangs. And Terri was unbelievably sweet. She has no backbone, except for once in the story and that didn't last too long. I have a very strong feeling that if I hadn't been familiar with the characters I would've given up on this book long before hitting page </span>
  <span id="freeText12428149646513495419" style="display:none">Really all my feelings on this book can be summed up in one large groan. I had been looking forward to reading about Bastien too. Bastien really could've been an interesting character, but Sands made him out to be a soft snuggle bunny with fangs. And Terri was unbelievably sweet. She has no backbone, except for once in the story and that didn't last too long. I have a very strong feeling that if I hadn't been familiar with the characters I would've given up on this book long before hitting page 100. This is the fourth book in the series and is pretty much just riding on the coat tails of Single White Vampire the whole time. The main plot of the story revolved around Luc and Kate's wedding. Kate's cousin, Terri, comes for the wedding and conveniently Kate gets called away on business leaving her cousin to sit around for a week with only Bastien for company. During that week disasters occur with the wedding plans which Terri and Bastien end up having to fix. If you're going to read this series I'd say it's pretty safe to skip this one. </span>
  <a data-text-id="12428149646513495419" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('BKlII5+PbY0eUF91NHBtS1n6x3WoItzn5jf9YV4Q631Stf3kEreOmlE1jeqAX2kiLvSQ9WvO7be+S0k+70VhVw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('XjeiN/kB/UyPXOW/Vo1hUHpmDRmeSHzo7Hbirgeh6uEIKxfwdDkeW8A5NyDiomU5DWhamV2kTbi0ClbxtvRgyw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer12348671192307803771">LYNSAY SANDS is the nationally bestselling author who is known for her hysterical historicals as well as the popular Argeneau/Rogue Hunter vampire series. With her witty and charming personality, Sands describes books as, “Waking dreams or stories, tales to amuse, entertain and distract us from everyday life.” She’s been writing stories since grade school and considers herself incredibly lucky to </span>
  <span id="freeText12348671192307803771" style="display:none">LYNSAY SANDS is the nationally bestselling author who is known for her hysterical historicals as well as the popular Argeneau/Rogue Hunter vampire series. With her witty and charming personality, Sands describes books as, “Waking dreams or stories, tales to amuse, entertain and distract us from everyday life.” She’s been writing stories since grade school and considers herself incredibly lucky to be able to make a career out of it. Her hope is that readers can get away from their everyday stress through her stories, and if there are occasional uncontrollable fits of laughter, that’s just a big bonus. Visit her official website at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.lynsaysands.net">www.lynsaysands.net</a>.<br /><br /></span>
